 ?" The boys who are sitting alone, or walking in groups, are the first to notice these policemen
 
 
 ek gali main apni motorcycle par akele baithe niraj ko inamen se paanch pulisavaalon ne 'gher' liya, or police adhikari ne sawaal daaga, "yahaan kyon baithe ho

 ?" Burbate-se Neeraj replied, "I work in a nearby restaurant
 
 
 ", or bataaya ki uski shift abhi-abhi khatm hui he, so, ghar lautne se pehle kuch der saans lenaa chahta hum
 
 
 The policeman, who checked Neeraj's Aadhaar card, said Gurrakar, "there is no need to sit here unnecessarily
 
 
 " sade kapade pahane ekh anya pulisavaale ne apane mobile phone se niraj kii tasviir khinchi, or jab unhen tasalli ho gai ki koi 'gadabad' nahin he, na ho sakati he, ve aage bad gaye
 
 
 Neeraj was shaken by this incident, and he refused to even talk to us
 
 
 
 
 
 And, shortly afterwards, things take an aggressive turn in the anti-romeo campaign
 
 
 dukaanon ke ek block ke saath pulisavaale saad khan ko gher lete hai, jo ek bench par akele baitha he
 
 
 Saad told the police that he had come with his wife, who was shopping at the women's clothing store
 
 
 ek varisht police adhikari kii ore se sawaal daaga jaataa he, "tum dukaan main bheetar kyon nahin gaye
 
 
 ? "before Saad is able to answer, his wife Nazira comes out of the store, and says to the husband" Come, let's go
 
 
 " The policemen immediately proceed, but Nazira is filled with anger by then
 
 
 "ise pareshaan karnaa kehete hai
 
 
 It cannot go with us within every shop
 
 
 yah dukaan mahilaon ke liye hai
 
 
 You cannot ask them why they are sitting here
 
 
 agar yah sharafat se dukaan ke baahar khadey hai, to isamen pareshaani kya he
 
 
 ? " haal hi main chunaav main shandaar jeet hasil kar sattashin hui bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ke chunavi vaadon main se ek 'anti-romeo squad' kii shuruyaat buudhvaar ko kuch galat ho gai, jab tivi par dikh rahi tasveeron main pulisavaalon ko yuva jodon or group main gum rahe purushon ko pareshaan karte dekha gaya
 
 
 Newly appointed Chief Minister Yogi Adityanath then had to direct that the couples should not be targeted
 
 
 baharhaal, yah saaf nahin he ki police ke paas saarvajanik sthanon par 'romeo' ko pakadaney ke liye kya yojana he, lekin philhal ek police adhikari ke mutabik, unka iraadaa "collejon or anya jagahon par akele or grupon main gum rahe ladakon se sawaal karne or unki jaanch karne kaa he, taaki chhedchhad kaa iraadaa rakhane waalon ke man main bhi dar paidaa ho
 
 
 " pulisavaalon kaa yah group isi bazaar main lagbhag 30 minute or bitaata he, lekin koi 'romeo' haath nahin aata

 This shop is for women
 
 
 aap inase nahin puch sakate ki yah yahaan kyon baithe hai
 
 
 If they are standing outside the shop with sharafat, then what is the problem? 
 
 ?" The anti-romeo Squad, one of the election promises of the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP), which was swept to power in the recent elections, went wrong on Wednesday, when the pictures seen on TV showed policemen to young couples and The men walking in the group were seen harassing
 
 
 navaniyukt mukhyamantri yogi adityanath ko iske baad nirdesh dena padaa ki jodon ko nishaanaa nahin banaaya jaae
 
 
 However, it is not clear what the police have plans to catch 'romeo' in public places, but according to a police officer at the moment, he intends to "question boys walking alone and in groups in colleges and elsewhere" And to investigate them, so that fear of those who intend to molest also be feared
 
 
 " This group of policemen spend about 30 more minutes in this market, but no 'romeo' hands
 
 
 kisi ko bhi hiraasat main nahin liya gaya
 
 
 The comments is team main maujuud varishthatam police adhikari shivaram yadav hamen samajhane kii koshish karte hai ki kyon ve akele paae ja rahe purushon se poochtacha kar rahe hai
 
 
 "we ask, is it wrong
 
 
 ? kya kisi se yah poochna galat he ki vah akelaa kyon gum rahaa he
 
 
 The If he came to the store, that's fine
 
 
 lekin akele ghoomane kaa kya matlab he
 
 
 The i can't understand why you would want to sit alone
 
 
 aap yahaan ek makasad - kharidari - se aae hai na
 
 
 ? "

 ' According to ICAR, 'green revolution wheat and paddy species are able to produce good only in conditions of high water and fertilizer and do not have the ability to withstand drought, flood, salt and heat
 ' genhu main sookhaa sahane vaale jin kii pahchaan ke liye puraani sookhaa avarodhi prajati si 306 tathaa nai harith kranti kii prajati dablyooel 711 kaa sankaran karke jinom ke un hisson kii pahchaan kar lee gai he, jisase jadon main vruddhi acchhee hoti he or kam pani main paidaavaar ho sakati he
 The need for a second Green Revolution has been underlined by experts in this scenario

 33 karod rupee kharch kiye or isi avadhi main udiessi ne 7
 51 crore was spent for this purpose
 artiai ke tahat isiear se mili jaankaree ke anusaar, jinom kii jaankaree praapt hone se gehun ankuran kii gati lagbhag doguni ho jaaegi

 Wave: Waves can be mainly divided into two parts: (i) mechanical wave (ii) non-mechanical wave (i) mechanical wave: waves that are in a physical medium (solid , Fluid, or gas), is called mechanical waves
 yantric tarangon ko mukhyatah do bhaagon main baanta gaya he:(a)anudaidhary tarang (longitudinal wave):jab tarang gati kii disha madhyam ke kanon ke kampan karne kii disha ke samaantar hoti he, to aisi tarang ko anudaidhary tarang kehete he
 Sound is an example of a non-responsive wave
 (b)anuprastha tarang (transverse wave):jab tarang gati kii disha madhyam ke kanon ke compann karne kii disha ke lambavat hoti he, to is prakaar kii tarangon ko anuprastha tarang kehete hai
 (ii) Electromagnetic waves: Waves that do not require any medium for transmission, ie waves can also be transmitted in vacuum, called electromagnetic or inertial waves: all electric
 Magnetic waves move at the same speed, which is equal to the speed of light
 sabhi vidyut chumbakeey tarangen photone kii bani hoti hai
 The wavelength complex of electromagnetic waves is 10 ^ -14 m
 se lekar 10^4me

 (b) It is transverse
 (c)yah prakaash ke veg se gaman hoti he
 (d) It has energy and momentum
 (e)isaki avadharana maxwell ke dwaara pratipaadit kii gai he

 (iii) electromagnetic waves: ultraviolet rays
 Complex: 10 ^ -8m to 10 ^ -7m Frequency Complex Hz: 10 ^ 16 to 10 ^ 14 Usage: Used in fomenting, emitting light-electrical effect, destroying bacteria

 9 x 10 ^ -7m to 7
 8 x10^-7m takaavriti parisar Hz:10^14 se 10^12 takaupyog: isse hamen vasteen dikhalaai padati hai

 8 x 10^-7m se 10^-3m takaavriti parisar Hz: 10^12 se 10^10takaupyog: ye kirane ushniya vikiran he, ye jis vastu par padati he, uskaa taap bad jaataa he

 The combination of Verb and Preposition, Verb and Adverb, Adverb and Preposition with Verb is called Phrasal Verb
 Phrasal varb kaa arth uski original varb ke arth se kaaphi alag hota he
 We often read only the first word, rather than read Phrasal Verb
 is tarah ham pehle shabd se hi vaakya kaa arth nikaalte hai or kanphyus hote hai
 Let's know about some similar Phrasal verbs of a alphabet: These 10 mistakes are often in English Ache for: Ache means pain, sorrow, pain
 lekin Phrasal varbayaachhe forka malatabaiachhese bilkul alag he
 Phrasal verb ache for means to crave or crave for something or human being
 aap ise or acchhee tarah se is udhaaharan se samaj sakate hai: She was lonely andaching forlove
 That is, she was alone and longing for love
 Abide by:is Phrasal varb kaa arth hota he aadar karnaa, ajna kaa paalan karnaa
 For example: i don't need to rule by the rules
 
 That is, i do not need to follow the rules
 Account for:account shabd kaa matlab hota he khaataa
 But Phrasal Verb Account for means to give reasons and answer
 udhaaharan ke liye: He was brought before the Board toaccount forhis behaviour
 That is, he was presented before the board to answer his attitude
 Act on:act shabd kaa arth hota he adhinium, abhinay karnaa, naatak karnaa, kaam karnaa
 But Act on Phrasal Verb means action after some result or else effect, effect, take action
 udhaaharan ke liye The policeacted onthe call they received
 Police started proceedings after the call
 Act out:phrasal varb act out ke do matlab hote hai:(1)abhinay yaa haav-bhav se kuch parform karnaa
 For example: Theyacted outthe story on stage
 yani ki unhone stage par abhinay ke jariye kahani bayaan kii
 (2) To express feelings by their behavior
 udhaaharan ke liye: Their anger isacted outin their antisocial behaviour
 That is, his anger is shown by his antisocial attitude
 Act up:is Phrasal varb kaa arth hota he buree tarah yaa ajeeb bartaav karnaa
 For example (1) Sophie got bored and startedacting up
 yani ki sophy bor ho gai or usne bura bartaav karnaa shuru kar diya
 (2) My computer'sacting up; i think i might have a virus
 yani ki meraa computer ajeeb dhang se kaam kar rahaa he, mujhe lagata he ki isamen virus aa gaya he
 (3) My head has startedacting upagain
 i need to get it examined
 That means my head has started to ache again
 mujhe jaanch karwaani hogi
 Answer back, Answer for, Answer to: All three are Phrasal Verbs
 answer backka matlab hota he palat ke jawaab dena,answer forka matlab hota he, kisi ke liye jimmedaar hona or kisi kii taraf se bolnaa aurainster toka matlab hota he uttaradaayi hona
 For example (1) Don'tanswer backyour elders
 yani ki apane se bado ko jawaab mat do
 (2) i agree, but i can't answer for my brother
 yani ki main aapaki baat se sahamat hum lekin main apane bhai kii taraf se kuch kah nahin saktaa
 (3) Thief will have toanswer tothe police
 yani ki chor ko police ko jawaab dena hoga
 Ask after: This Phrasal verb means to ask about one's well-being
 jaise ki My Sister is alwaysasking afteryou
 That is, my sister always asks about you
 Ask in:iskaa matlab hota he kisi ko andar aane ke liye poochna
 For example: Ravi at the door
 ' 'askhimin
 That is, Ravi is at the door, ask him to come inside
 Ask out:iskaa matlab hota he kisi se baahar chalane ke liye poochna
 For example: He wanted toaskheroutbut was too shy
 yani ki vah usase baahar chalane ke liye poochna chahta tha, lekin use shame aa rahi thi
 The government has taken steps to locate the 87 companies and their directors, which disappeared overnight after raising funds from the public
 gujarat is maamle main sabase aage he or vahaan aisi companiyon kii sankhya 26 he
 There are 13 companies in Andhra Pradesh, 10 in Tamil Nadu, nine in Maharashtra, five each in Delhi, West Bengal and Madhya Pradesh and four each in Uttar Pradesh and Bihar
 chandigarh or karnataka main do-do tathaa punjab or odisha main ek-ek aisi company he
 According to the details prepared by the Ministry of Company Affairs, an FIR has been lodged against such companies and their directors in the police of the respective state
 adhikariyon ne kaha ki aisi companiyon kii talash kar unke khilaaf uchit karrwai kii jaaegi
 After the raising of capital, if the offices and directors of a company are not known, they are classified as missing
 tippaniyan According to the Corporate Affairs document, lawsuits have been filed against these companies, their promoters and directors under the Companies Act
 in companiyon par vaidhanik ritern nahin daakhil karne, prospectos main juthi soochna dene or janata se dhokhadhadi kar unhen dhan nivesh ke liye prerit karne kaa aarope he

 The committee has also suggested ways to assess the e-flow of the river's environment, and the Minimum Environment requirement-mer
 inamen se ek ahm suzav ye he ki nadi par ashrith un khaas jeev jantuon kii pahchaan kii jaae jo nadi kii puri yatra ke dauraan uske swasth hone kaa indicater maane ja sakate hai
 As such, snow trout and golden Mahaseer fishes in the Upper Ganges basin have been considered as such indicators in this report
 nadi ke puure uthle or gahare raste main saal ke alag-alag mausamon main kahaan kitna pani banaae rakhkar aise jeev jantuon kii prajati ko bachaae or badaye rakhaa ja saktaa he usee ke aadhaar par i flo or MER ko tay kiya janaa chahie
 The report has divided the health of the river into five sections
 moulik, moulik ke qareeb, thodaa prabhavit, kaafii prabhavit or vikrut rup
 If the river flow is less than the minimum environmental requirement (MER), it is in a distorted form
 bharat main zyaadaatar nadiyaan (uttar purv or himalay ke upree cachament kii kuch nadiyon ko chhodkar) vikrut rup main hai kyonki unamem nunatam bahaav bhi nahin he
 If the flow of a river is equal to its average flow over the years, then the river should be considered as its original form
 cameti ke mutabik nadi main pani kaa i flo uske MER yani nunatam paryaavarniya zarurat se zyaada hona chahie taaki wo apni moulik bhoomika ko nibhaati rah sake
 But this description of the health of the river is more than the amount of its water
 pani kii quality, uske jaivik gun vagairah par baaten tay honi abhi baaki hai
 The comments report ke mutabik pani kaa nunatam bahaav banaae rakhana nadi hi nahin logon or samaaj kii bhi zarurat he
 If this minimum extent is not maintained, then the distorted form of the river will end its ecosystem, which will have a far-reaching effect on human society too soon
 jane-maane paryaavaranvid himanshu thakkar kaa maananaa he ki apane hi jal sansaadhan mantralay kii banaai cameti kii is sabase tazaa report ko hi agar sarkaar gambhirtha se le or supreme court main apane rukh ko sudhaar le to use apane saamne khadey kai kathin sawaalon ke jawaab khud hi mil jaaenge
 The implementation of the report can open not only the Ganges but also the way to make the rivers across the country clean and continuous
 report ke mutabik nadi kaa i-flo hi uske pani kii quality or usamen maujuud jaleey jivan ko nirdhaarit karata he
 The e-flow of the river will also prove to be the foundation for sustaining spiritual, cultural activities and will be the backbone of river-based jobs and enterprises
 nadi kaa i-flo sirf pani ke bahaav tak hi simit nahin he balki ye pani ke saath aage jane vaale cediment yani gaad kii maatra ko bhi tay karata he

 isiilie cameti kii report main is baat par jor diya gaya he ki kisi bhi pariyojna ke banane ke baad bhi nadi main pani or gaad kaa santulan vaisaa hi bane rahanaa chahie jaisaa bina kisi baadha yaa baandh ke tha

 ) Six months have passed since the academic sessions of government schools in Jharkhand started, and for the past several months, children have been asking the same question, when will they get the books? The plan of the government to provide free books to poor children in the state government schools from class one to eight is that the education department took nine months to complete the first tender process, under which many publishers were nearly 45 crores Rs
 kii kitabon ke prakaashan kaa order diya tha
 But due to the sluggish pace of the department and the negligence of the publishers, the students are yet to get the books
 haalanki prakashkon ko yah nirdesh diya gaya tha ki ve supplai kaa kaam 10 agast tak puraa kar len
 When the National Commission for Protection of Child Rights (NCPCR) called on the state government to respond to the matter, the government and publishers claimed the entire allocation by simply supplying books to a few schools
 lekin maatr duusari kaksha ke chaatro ke bich kitabon kaa aavanton hua, vah bhi aadha adhuraa
 Yes, the delay has benefited the publishers since the game of publishing the first tender on September last year and then canceling it thrice was Rs 45 crore
 kii laagat vaali is yojana kii laagat 79 karod ru
 happened
